It supports unlimited staves with up to four voices each, dynamics, articulations, lyrics, chords, lead sheet notation, import/export of MIDI and MusicXML, export to PDF and WAV, plus online score sharing.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can upload scores directly to the score sharing site musescore.com.
